            <script>
             $(document).ready(function(){
 var init = false;
 $(".input-event-date").each(function(i,v){
 var $v = $(v);
 $v.datepicker({
 altField: "#" + $v.attr("data-target"),
 altFormat: "yy-mm-dd",
 beforeShow: function(){
 if (!init) {
 console.log("before");
 init = true;
 $("#ui-datepicker-div").click(function(e){
 e.stopPropagation();
 });
 }
 }
 });
 });
 var search = $(".eventSearch"),
 form = search.find("form"),
 submitClick = form.find(".submited");
 submitClick.unbind().click(function(event){
 event.preventDefault();
 var get_action = "/en/events/events/events.html";
 var hashData = buildHash(),
 hashUrl = get_action+hashData,
 oldUrl = String(document.location),
 newUrl = hashUrl;
 console.log("hashUrl URL: "+hashUrl);
 console.log("Old URL: "+oldUrl);
 console.log("New URL: "+newUrl);
 // categories
 var categories = form.find(".eventCheckBox:checked").map(function(){
 return $(this).val();
 }).get();
 if(categories && categories.length) {
 newUrl = newUrl + "/category/" + encodeURIComponent(categories.join(","));
 }
 window.location.href = newUrl;
 });
 /* Submit by Enter */
 form.keydown(function(e) {
 if (e.keyCode == 13) {
 //form.submit();
 submitClick.trigger("click");
 }
 });
 var buildHash = function(){
 var data = updateHashData();
 if (data.event && data.action) {
 var s = "#!/" + data.event +"/"+ data.action;
 if (data.data) {
 var options = []
 for (var i in data.data) {
 options.push(i +"/"+ data.data[i]);
 }
 if (options.length) {
 s += "/" + options.join("/");
 }
 }
 return s;
 }
 };
 var updateHashData = function() {
 var objects = form.find(".hash-field").serializeArray(),
 data = {};
 data.event = "event"; // controller
 data.action = "search"; // action
 data.data = {};
 console.log("objects");
 console.log(objects);
 $.each(objects, function(key, obj ) {
 if (obj.value) {
 data.data[obj.name] = obj.value;
 }
 });
 console.log(data);
 return data;
 };
 });
            </script>

        <div class="modal modal-dark fade overlayVideoInteractive" id="videoInteractiveOverlay" role="dialog" tabindex="-1">
         <div class="modal-dialog" role="document">
          <div class="modal-content">
           <div class="modal-header">
            <button aria-label="Close" class="close" data-dismiss="modal" type="button">
             <span aria-hidden="true" class="dzt dzt-16 dzt-close-16">
             </span>
            </button>
           </div>
           <div class="modal-body">
            <div class="iframe-wrap">
             <iframe class="iframe-video-interactive" data-src="/en/germany-at-night.html" scrolling="no">
             </iframe>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>

        <script>
         jQuery(function($){
 var
 modal = $("#videoInteractiveOverlay"),
 iframe = $(".iframe-video-interactive"),
 li = $("#nav899991"),
 button = li.find("a");
 modal.modal({
 show: false
 });
 modal.on("hidden.modal.bs", function(e){
 iframe.attr("src", "");
 });
 button.unbind().on("click", function(e){
 e.preventDefault();
 modal.modal("show");
 iframe.attr("src", iframe.data("src"));
 });
 modal.on("click", "button.close", function(e){
 e.preventDefault();
 iframe.attr("src", "");
 modal.modal("hide");
 });
 });
        </script>

 			var

 				abbreviation	= optionSelected.attr("value"),

 					case "hk":
 						abbrLang = "hk";
 						l		 = "cn";
 						currTrans= translation["cn"];
 						break;
 					case "be-fr":
 						abbrLang = "be";
 						l		 = "fr";
 						currTrans= translation["fr"];
 						break;
 					case "ca-fr":
 						abbrLang = "ca";
 						l		 = "fr";
 						currTrans= translation["fr"];
 						break;
 					case "cn-en":
 						abbrLang = "cn";
 						l		 = "en";
 						currTrans= translation["en"];
 						break;
 					case "ar":
 						abbrLang = "ar";
 						l		 = "es";
 						currTrans= translation["es"];
 						break;
 					case "cl":
 						abbrLang = "cl";
 						l		 = "es";
 						currTrans= translation["es"];
 						break;
 					case "mx":
 						abbrLang = "mx";
 						l		 = "es";
 						currTrans= translation["es"];
 						break;
 					default: 
 						abbrLang = abbreviation;
 						currTrans= translation[abbrLang] ? translation[abbrLang]: translation["en"];
 						break;
 				}
 			var
 				countryName		= optionSelected.data().country,
 				data			= {},
 				form			= $(this).closest("form");	
 			currTrans["country_name"]	= countryName;
 			currTrans["country_abbr"]	= abbreviation;
 				currTrans["countryList"] = countryList;
 			$.each(form.serializeArray(), function() {
 			    data[this.name] = this.value;
 			});
 			currTrans["data"] = data;
 			headline.find(".news-country").html(" ( " + countryName+ " )");
 			wrap.html(selectTpl(currTrans));	
 			if("archiv" in window) {
 				archiv.render(abbrLang, l);
 			}
 		});
 		wrap.on("click", "form.newsletter .submit", function(e) {		
 			var 
 				valid			= true,
 				form			= wrap.find("form"),
 				containerError	= wrap.find(".container-error"),
 				loader			= wrap.find(".loader"),
 				newsConfirm		= wrap.find(".confirmation")
 				;			
 			e.preventDefault();
 			wrap.find(".mandatory").each(function(i,v) {
 				var
 					$v				= $(v),
 					val 			= $v.val(),
 					data 			= $v.data(),
 					def 			= data.preset,
 					type 			= $v.attr("type"),
 					classError 		= "error",
 					classFilled 	= "postfill",
 					label 			= wrap.find("." + data.label);
 				if (type == "checkbox") {
 					if ($v.is(":checked")) {
 						label.removeClass(classError);
 					} else {
 						valid = false;
 						label.addClass(classError);
 					}
 				} else if($v.is("select")) {
 					if(val == null) {
 						$v.addClass(classError);
 						valid = false;
 					} else {
 						$v.removeClass(classError);
 					}
 				}
 				else {
 					var checkValid = true;
 					try {
 						if (data.validator) {
 							var xp = new RegExp(data.validator.slice(1, -1));
 							checkValid = xp.test(val);
 						}
 					} catch (e) {}
 					if ( !checkValid || (val !== null && def !== null && val === def) || (val !== null && $.trim(val.length) < 1) ) {
 						valid = false;
 						$v.addClass(classError);
 						label.addClass(classError);
 						if($v.hasClass("dx-select")) {
 							$v.closest(".dropdown")
 								.find(".dropdown-toggle")
 								.addClass(classError);
 						}
 					} else {
 						$v.removeClass(classError);
 						label.removeClass(classError);
 						if($v.hasClass("dx-select")) {
 							$v.closest(".dropdown")
 								.find(".dropdown-toggle")
 								.removeClass(classError);
 						}
 					}
 				}
 			});
 			if(!valid) {
 				containerError.slideDown();
 				$("html,body").animate({scrollTop: $(".container-error").offset().top});
 			} else {
 				containerError.slideUp();
 				loader.show();
 				$.post("/applications/jproxy.php", {url: "/lottery/index/track", data:form.serialize()}, function(data) {
 					if(data && data.success && data.success == true) {
 						form.slideUp();
 						loader.hide(); 
 						newsConfirm.slideDown();
 						if("application" in window) {
 							application.msg.notify("wkl-send-success");
 						}
 					} else {
 						loader.hide();
 						alert("An error has occured, please try again later!");
 					}
 				});
 			}
 		});
 	});
       </script>

   <script>
    (function(){
 	var
 		key = "cookieNotice",
 		run = function(){
 			
 			if ("localStorage" in window && key in localStorage) {
 				return;
 			}
 			
 			if ("jQuery" in window && "application" in window && "tpl" in application) {
 				
 				try {
 					var tpl = application.tpl("cookieSnippet");
 					if (tpl) {
 						$("body")
 							.on("click", ".cookie-snippet button", function(e){
 								e.preventDefault();
 								localStorage[key] = "1";
 								$(".cookie-snippet").remove();
 							})					
 							.append(tpl({}));
 					}
 				} catch (e) {
 					console.error("cookie snippet error");
 				}
 			} else {
 				console.error("cannot run cookie snippet - jQuery/application/tpl missing");
 			}
 		};
 	
 	if ("_queue" in window) {
 		_queue.push(run);
 	} else if ("jQuery" in window) {
 		jQuery(run);
 	} else {
 		document.onload = run;
 	}
 })();
   </script>
